class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Bigfalls14w_info.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         The\n         <a href="/wiki/Great_Falls_(Passaic_River)" title="Great Falls (Passaic River)">\n          Great Falls\n         </a>\n         of the\n         <a href="/wiki/Passaic_River" title="Passaic River">\n          Passaic River\n         </a>\n         in\n         <a href="/wiki/Paterson,_New_Jersey" title="Paterson, New Jersey">\n          Paterson\n         </a>\n         , dedicated as a\n         <a href="/wiki/List_of_national_parks_of_the_United_States" title="List of national parks of the United States">\n          U.S. National Park\n         </a>\n         in November 2011, incorporates one of the largest\n         <a href="/wiki/Waterfall" title="Waterfall">\n          waterfalls\n         </a>\n         in the eastern United States.\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-53">\n          <a href="#cite_note-53">\n           [53]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Geography_of_New_Jersey" title="Geography of New Jersey">\n        Geography of New Jersey\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       See also:\n       <a href="/wiki/List_of_counties_in_New_Jersey" title="List of counties in New Jersey">\n        List of counties in New Jersey\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Metropolitan_Statistical_Areas_of_New_Jersey" title="Metropolitan Statistical Areas of New Jersey">\n        Metropolitan Statistical Areas of New Jersey\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       New Jersey is bordered on the north and northeast by New York (parts of which are across the\n       <a href="/wiki/Hudson_River" title="Hudson River">\n        Hudson River\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Upper_New_York_Bay" title="Upper New York Bay">\n        Upper New York Bay\n       </a>\n       , the\n       <a href="/wiki/Kill_Van_Kull" title="Kill Van Kull">\n        Kill Van Kull\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Newark_Bay" title="Newark Bay">\n        Newark Bay\n       </a>\n       , and the\n       <a href="/wiki/Arthur_Kill" title="Arthur Kill">\n        Arthur Kill\n       </a>\n       ); on the east by the Atlantic Ocean; on the southwest by\n       <a href="/wiki/Delaware" title="Delaware">\n        Delaware\n       </a>\n       across\n       <a href="/wiki/Delaware_Bay" title="Delaware Bay">\n        Delaware Bay\n       </a>\n       ; and on the west by\n       <a href="/wiki/Pennsylvania" title="Pennsylvania">\n        Pennsylvania\n       </a>\n       across the\n       <a href="/wiki/Delaware_River" title="Delaware River">\n        Delaware River\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       New Jersey can be thought of as five regions, based upon natural geography and population concentration. Northeastern New Jersey, the\n       <a href="/wiki/Gateway_Region" title="Gateway Region">\n        Gateway Region\n       </a>\n       , lies closest to\n       <a href="/wiki/Manhattan" title="Manhattan">\n        Manhattan\n       </a>\n       in New York City, and up to a million residents commute daily into the city to work via automobile or\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mass_transit" title="Mass transit">\n        mass transit\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-54">\n        <a href="#cite_note-54">\n         [54]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Northwestern New Jersey, or the "\n       <a href="/wiki/Skylands_Region" title="Skylands Region">\n        Skylands\n       </a>\n       ", is, compared to the northeast, more wooded, rural, and mountainous. The "\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Jersey_shore" title="Jersey shore">\n        Shore\n       </a>\n       ", along the Atlantic Coast in the central-east and southeast, has its own natural, residential, and lifestyle characteristics owing to its location by the ocean. The\n       <a href="/wiki/Delaware_Valley" title="Delaware Valley">\n        Delaware Valley\n       </a>\n       includes the southwestern counties of the state, which reside within the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Philadelphia_Metropolitan_Area" title="Philadelphia Metropolitan Area">\n        Philadelphia Metropolitan Area\n       </a>\n       . The fifth region is the\n       <a href="/wiki/Pine_Barrens_(New_Jersey)" title="Pine Barrens (New Jersey)">\n        Pine Barrens\n       </a>\n       in the interior of the southern part. Covered rather extensively by mixed\n       <a href="/wiki/Pine" title="Pine">\n        pine\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Oak" title="Oak">\n        oak\n       </a>\n       forest, it has a much lower population density than much of the rest of the state.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       New Jersey also can be broadly divided into three geographic regions:\n       <a href="/wiki/North_Jersey" title="North Jersey">\n        North Jersey\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Central_Jersey" title="Central Jersey">\n        Central Jersey\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/South_Jersey" title="South Jersey">\n        South Jersey\n       </a>\n       . Some New Jersey residents do not consider Central Jersey a region in its own right, but others believe it is a separate geographic and cultural area from the North and South.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The federal\n       <a href="/wiki/Office_of_Management_and_Budget" title="Office of Management and Budget">\n        Office of Management and Budget\n       </a>\n       divides New Jersey\'s counties into seven\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Metropolitan_Statistical_Area" title="Metropolitan Statistical Area">\n        Metropolitan Statistical Areas\n       </a>\n       , including sixteen counties in the New York City or Philadelphia metro areas. Four counties have independent metro areas, and Warren County is part of the Pennsylvania-based\n       <a href="/wiki/Lehigh_Valley" title="Lehigh Valley">\n        Lehigh Valley\n       </a>\n       metro area. It is also at the center of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Northeast_megalopolis" title="Northeast megalopolis">\n        Northeast megalopolis\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Additionally, the New Jersey Commerce, Economic Growth, &amp; Tourism Commission divides the state into six distinct regions to facilitate the state\'s tourism industry. The regions are:\n      </p>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Gateway_Region" title="Gateway Region">\n         Gateway Region\n        </a>\n        , encompassing\n        <a href="/wiki/Middlesex_County,_New_Jersey" title="Middlesex County, New Jersey">\n         Middlesex County\n        </a>\n        ,\n        <a href="/wiki/Union_County,_New_Jersey" title="Union County, New Jersey">\n         Union County\n        </a>\n        ,\n        <a href="/wiki/Essex_County,_New_Jersey" title="Essex County, New Jersey">\n         Essex County\n        </a>\n        ,\n        <a href="/wiki/Hudson_County,_New_Jersey" title="Hudson County, New Jersey">\n         Hudson County\n        </a>\n        ,\n        <a href="/wiki/Bergen_County,_New_Jersey" title="Bergen County, New Jersey">\n         Bergen County\n        </a>\n        , and\n        <a href="/wiki/Passaic_County,_New_Jersey" title="Passaic County, New Jersey">\n         Passaic County\n        </a>\n        .\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Skylands_Region" title="Skylands Region">\n         Skylands Region\n        </a>\n        , encompassing\n        <a href="/wiki/Sussex_County,_New_Jersey" title="Sussex County, New Jersey">\n         Sussex County\n        </a>\n        ,\n        <a href="/wiki/Morris_County,_New_Jersey" title="Morris County, New Jersey">\n         Morris County\n        </a>\n        ,\n        <a href="/wiki/Warren_County,_New_Jersey" title="Warren County, New Jersey">\n         Warren County\n        </a>\n        ,\n        <a href="/wiki/Hunterdon_County,_New_Jersey" title="Hunterdon County, New Jersey">\n         Hunterdon County\n        </a>\n        , and\n        <a href="/wiki/Somerset_County,_New_Jersey" title="Somerset County, New Jersey">\n         Somerset County\n        </a>\n        .\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Shore_Region" title="Shore Region">\n         Shore Region\n        </a>\n        , encompassing\n        <a href="/wiki/Monmouth_County,_New_Jersey" title="Monmouth County, New Jersey">\n         Monmouth County\n        </a>\n        and\n        <a href="/wiki/Ocean_County,_New_Jersey" title="Ocean County, New Jersey">\n         Ocean County\n        </a>\n        .\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Delaware_River_Region" title="Delaware River Region">\n         Delaware River Region\n        </a>\n        , encompassing\n        <a href="/wiki/Mercer_County,_New_Jersey" title="Mercer County, New Jersey">\n         Mercer County\n        </a>\n        ,\n        <a href="/wiki/Burlington_County,_New_Jersey" title="Burlington County, New Jersey">\n         Burlington County\n        </a>\n        ,\n        <a href="/wiki/Camden_County,_New_Jersey" title="Camden County, New Jersey">\n         Camden County\n        </a>\n        ,\n        <a href="/wiki/Gloucester_County,_New_Jersey" title="Gloucester County, New Jersey">\n         Gloucester County\n        </a>\n        , and\n        <a href="/wiki/Salem_County,_New_Jersey" title="Salem County, New Jersey">\n         Salem County\n        </a>\n        .\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Greater_Atlantic_City_Region" title="Greater Atlantic City Region">\n         Greater Atlantic City Region\n        </a>\n        , encompassing\n        <a href="/wiki/Atlantic_County,_New_Jersey" title="Atlantic County, New Jersey">\n         Atlantic County\n        </a>\n        .\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Southern_Shore_Region" title="Southern Shore Region">\n         Southern Shore Region\n        </a>\n        , encompassing\n        <a href="/wiki/Cumberland_County,_New_Jersey" title="Cumberland County, New Jersey">\n         Cumberland County\n        </a>\n        and\n        <a href="/wiki/Cape_May_County,_New_Jersey" title="Cape May County, New Jersey">\n         Cape May County\n        </a>\n        .\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <p>\n       <a href="/wiki/High_Point_(New_Jersey)" title="High Point (New Jersey)">\n        High Point\n       </a>\n       , in\n       <a href="/wiki/Montague_Township,_New_Jersey" title="Montague Township, New Jersey">\n        Montague Township\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Sussex_County,_New_Jersey" title="Sussex County, New Jersey">\n        Sussex County\n       </a>\n       , is the highest elevation, at 1,803 feet (550\xc2\xa0m). The\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/New_Jersey_Palisades" title="New Jersey Palisades">\n        Palisades\n       </a>\n       are a line of steep cliffs on the lower west side of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Hudson_River" title="Hudson River">\n        Hudson River\n       </a>\n       , in\n       <a href="/wiki/Bergen_County,_New_Jersey" title="Bergen County, New Jersey">\n        Bergen County\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Hudson_County,_New_Jersey" title="Hudson County, New Jersey">\n        Hudson County\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Major\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_New_Jersey_rivers" title="List of New Jersey rivers">\n        rivers\n       </a>\n       include the\n       <a href="/wiki/Hudson_River" title="Hudson River">\n        Hudson\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Delaware_River" title="Delaware River">\n        Delaware\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Raritan_River" title="Raritan River">\n        Raritan\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Passaic_River" title="Passaic River">\n        Passaic\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Hackensack_River" title="Hackensack River">\n        Hackensack\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Rahway_River" title="Rahway River">\n        Rahway\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Musconetcong_River" title="Musconetcong River">\n        Musconetcong\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Mullica_River" title="Mullica River">\n        Mullica\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Rancocas_River" title="Rancocas River">\n        Rancocas\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Manasquan_River" title="Manasquan River">\n        Manasquan\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Maurice_River" title="Maurice River">\n        Maurice\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Toms_River" title="Toms River">\n        Toms\n       </a>\n       rivers.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sandy_Hook_(New_Jersey)" title="Sandy Hook (New Jersey)">\n        Sandy Hook\n       </a>\n       , along the eastern coast, is a popular recreational beach. It is a barrier\n       <a href="/wiki/Spit_(landform)" title="Spit (landform)">\n        spit\n       </a>\n       and an extension of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Barnegat_Peninsula" title="Barnegat Peninsula">\n        Barnegat Peninsula\n       </a>\n       along the state\'s Atlantic Ocean coast.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       <a href="/wiki/Long_Beach_Island" title="Long Beach Island">\n        Long Beach Island\n       </a>\n       ("LBI"), a\n       <a href="/wiki/Barrier_island" title="Barrier island">\n        barrier island\n       </a>\n       along the eastern coast, has popular recreational beaches. The primary access point to the island is by a single bridge connection to the mainland.\n       <a href="/wiki/Barnegat_Lighthouse" title="Barnegat Lighthouse">\n        Barnegat Lighthouse\n       </a>\n       is on the northern tip.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Areas managed by the\n       <a href="/wiki/National_Park_Service" title="National Park Service">\n        National Park Service\n       </a>\n       include:\n      </p>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Appalachian_National_Scenic_Trail" title="Appalachian National Scenic Trail">\n         Appalachian National Scenic Trail\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Delaware_National_Scenic_River" title="Delaware National Scenic River">\n         Delaware National Scenic River\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Delaware_Water_Gap_National_Recreation_Area" title="Delaware Water Gap National Recreation Area">\n         Delaware Water Gap National Recreation Area\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ellis_Island_National_Monument" title="Ellis Island National Monument">\n         Ellis Island National Monument\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Gateway_National_Recreation_Area" title="Gateway National Recreation Area">\n         Gateway National Recreation Area\n        </a>\n        in Monmouth County\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Great_Egg_Harbor_River" title="Great Egg Harbor River">\n         Great Egg Harbor River\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Morristown_National_Historical_Park" title="Morristown National Historical Park">\n         Morristown National Historical Park\n        </a>\n        in\n        <a href="/wiki/Morristown,_New_Jersey" title="Morristown, New Jersey">\n         Morristown\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/New_Jersey_Coastal_Heritage_Trail_Route" title="New Jersey Coastal Heritage Trail Route">\n         New Jersey Coastal Heritage Trail Route\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/New_Jersey_Pinelands_National_Reserve" title="New Jersey Pinelands National Reserve">\n         New Jersey Pinelands National Reserve\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Paterson_Great_Falls_National_Historical_Park" title="Paterson Great Falls National Historical Park">\n         Paterson Great Falls National Historical Park\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Thomas_Edison_National_Historical_Park" title="Thomas Edison National Historical Park">\n         Thomas Edison National Historical Park\n        </a>\n        in\n        <a href="/wiki/West_Orange,_New_Jersey" title="West Orange, New Jersey">\n         West Orange\n        </a>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <p>\n       Prominent geographic features include:\n      </p>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Delaware_Water_Gap" title="Delaware Water Gap">\n         Delaware Water Gap\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Great_Bay_(New_Jersey)" title="Great Bay (New Jersey)">\n         Great Bay\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Great_Swamp_National_Wildlife_Refuge" title="Great Swamp National Wildlife Refuge">\n         Great Swamp National Wildlife Refuge\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/New_York%E2%80%93New_Jersey_Highlands" title="New York\xe2\x80\x93New Jersey Highlands">\n         Highlands\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hudson_Palisades" title="Hudson Palisades">\n         Hudson Palisades\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/New_Jersey_Meadowlands" title="New Jersey Meadowlands">\n         Meadowlands\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Pine_Barrens_(New_Jersey)" title="Pine Barrens (New Jersey)">\n         Pine Barrens\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/South_Mountain_Reservation" title="South Mountain Reservation">\n         South Mountain\n        </a>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Climate">\n        Climate\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:NJ_koppen.svg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1890" data-file-width="990" height="420" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/NJ_koppen.svg/220px-NJ_koppen.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/NJ_koppen.svg/330px-NJ_koppen.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/NJ_koppen.svg/440px-NJ_koppen.svg.png 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:NJ_koppen.svg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         K\xc3\xb6ppen climate types of New Jersey\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       There are two climatic conditions in the state. The south, central, and northeast parts of the state have a\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Humid_subtropical" title="Humid subtropical">\n        humid subtropical\n       </a>\n       climate, while the northwest has a\n       <a href="/wiki/Humid_continental_climate" title="Humid continental climate">\n        humid continental climate\n       </a>\n       (\n       <a href="/wiki/Microthermal" title="Microthermal">\n        microthermal\n       </a>\n       ), with much cooler temperatures due to higher elevation. New Jersey receives between 2,400 and 2,800 hours of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sunshine" title="Sunshine">\n        sunshine\n       </a>\n       annually.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-55">\n        <a href="#cite_note-55">\n         [55]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Summers are typically hot and humid, with statewide average high temperatures of 82\xe2\x80\x9387\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0F (28\xe2\x80\x9331\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0C) and lows of 60\xe2\x80\x9369\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0F (16\xe2\x80\x9321\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0C); however, temperatures exceed 90\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0F (32\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0C) on average 25 days each summer, exceeding 100\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0F (38\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0C) in some years. Winters are usually cold, with average high temperatures of 34\xe2\x80\x9343\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0F (1\xe2\x80\x936\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0C) and lows of 16 to 28\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0F (\xe2\x88\x929 to \xe2\x88\x922\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0C) for most of the state, but temperatures could, for brief periods, fall below 10\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0F (\xe2\x88\x9212\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0C) and occasionally rise above 50\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0F (10\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0C). Northwestern parts of the state have significantly colder winters with sub-0\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0F (\xe2\x88\x9218\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0C) being an almost annual occurrence. Spring and autumn may feature wide temperature variations, with lower humidity than summer. The\n       <a href="/wiki/Hardiness_zone" title="Hardiness zone">\n        USDA Plant Hardiness Zone\n       </a>\n       classification ranges from 6 in the northwest of the state, to 7B near Cape May.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-56">\n        <a href="#cite_note-56">\n         [56]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       All-time temperature extremes recorded in New Jersey include 110\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0F (43\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0C) on July 10, 1936 in\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Runyon,_New_Jersey" title="Runyon, New Jersey">\n        Runyon\n       </a>\n       , Middlesex County and \xe2\x88\x9234\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0F (\xe2\x88\x9237\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0C) on January 5, 1904 in\n       <a href="/wiki/River_Vale,_New_Jersey" title="River Vale, New Jersey">\n        River Vale\n       </a>\n       , Bergen County.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-57">\n        <a href="#cite_note-57">\n         [57]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Average annual precipitation ranges from 43 to 51 inches (1,100 to 1,300\xc2\xa0mm), uniformly spread through the year. Average snowfall per winter season ranges from 10\xe2\x80\x9315 inches (25\xe2\x80\x9338\xc2\xa0cm) in the south and near the seacoast, 15\xe2\x80\x9330 inches (38\xe2\x80\x9376\xc2\xa0cm) in the northeast and central part of the state, to about 40\xe2\x80\x9350 inches (1.0\xe2\x80\x931.3\xc2\xa0m) in the northwestern highlands, but this often varies considerably from year to year. Precipitation falls on an average of 120 days a year, with 25 to 30 thunderstorms, most of which occur during the summer.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       During winter and early spring, New Jersey can experience "\n       <a href="/wiki/Nor%27easter" title="Nor\'easter">\n        nor\'easters\n       </a>\n       ", which are capable of causing\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Blizzards" title="Blizzards">\n        blizzards\n       </a>\n       or flooding throughout the northeastern United States.\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hurricane" title="Hurricane">\n        Hurricanes\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tropical_storm" title="Tropical storm">\n        tropical storms\n       </a>\n       (such as Tropical Storm Floyd in 1999\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-58">\n        <a href="#cite_note-58">\n         [58]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       ),\n       <a href="/wiki/Tornado" title="Tornado">\n        tornadoes\n       </a>\n       , and earthquakes are rare, although New Jersey was severely impacted by\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Sandy" title="Hurricane Sandy">\n        Hurricane Sandy\n       </a>\n       on October 29, 2012 with the storm making landfall in the state at 90\xc2\xa0mph.\n      </p>\n      <table class="wikitable" style="text-align:center;font-size:90%;">\n       <tr>\n <br/>\n          2015 Estimate\n          <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-PopEstUS_63-0">\n           <a href="#cite_note-PopEstUS-63">\n            [63]\n           </a>\n          </sup>\n class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:New_Jersey_Population_Map.png" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         New Jersey population distribution\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="State_population">\n        State population\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States_Census_Bureau" title="United States Census Bureau">\n        United States Census Bureau\n       </a>\n       estimates that the population of New Jersey was 8,958,013 on July 1, 2015, a 1.89% increase since the\n       <a href="/wiki/2010_United_States_Census" title="2010 United States Census">\n        2010 United States Census\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-PopEstUS_63-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-PopEstUS-63">\n         [63]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Residents of New Jersey are most commonly referred to as "New Jerseyans" or, less commonly, as "New Jerseyites". As of the 2010 census, there were 8,791,894 people residing in the state. The racial makeup of the state was:\n      </p>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        68.6%\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/White_American" title="White American">\n         White American\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        13.7%\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/African_American" title="African American">\n         African American\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        8.3%\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Asian_American" title="Asian American">\n         Asian American\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        0.3%\n        <a href="/wiki/Native_Americans_in_the_United_States" title="Native Americans in the United States">\n         Native American\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        2.7%\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Multiracial_American" title="Multiracial American">\n         Multiracial American\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        6.4%\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Race_(U.S._Census)" title="Race (U.S. Census)">\n         other races\n        </a>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <p>\n       17.7% of the population were\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hispanic_(U.S._Census)" title="Hispanic (U.S. Census)">\n        Hispanic\n       </a>\n       or\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Latino_(U.S._Census)" title="Latino (U.S. Census)">\n        Latino\n       </a>\n       (of any race).\n      </p>\n      <table class="wikitable sortable collapsible" style="font-size: 90%;">\n       <caption>\n        <b>\n         New Jersey Racial Breakdown of Population\n        </b>\n       </caption>\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n         Racial composition\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         1970\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-census_64-0">\n          <a href="#cite_note-census-64">\n           [64]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         1990\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-census_64-1">\n          <a href="#cite_note-census-64">\n           [64]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         2000\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-65">\n          <a href="#cite_note-65">\n           [65]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         2010\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-66">\n          <a href="#cite_note-66">\n           [66]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n        </th>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/White_American" title="White American">\n          White\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         88.6%\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         79.3%\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         72.5%\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         68.6%\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/African_American" title="African American">\n          Black\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         10.7%\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         13.4%\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         13.6%\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         13.7%\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Asian_American" title="Asian American">\n          Asian\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         0.3%\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         3.5%\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         5.7%\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         8.3%\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/Native_Americans_in_the_United_States" title="Native Americans in the United States">\n          Native\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         0.1%\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         0.2%\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         0.2%\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         0.3%\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Native_Hawaiian" title="Native Hawaiian">\n          Native Hawaiian\n         </a>\n         and\n         <br/>\n         <a href="/wiki/Pacific_Islander" title="Pacific Islander">\n          other Pacific Islander\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         \xe2\x80\x93\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         \xe2\x80\x93\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         \xe2\x80\x93\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         \xe2\x80\x93\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n 0.3%\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         3.6%\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         5.4%\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         6.4%\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Multiracial_American" title="Multiracial American">\n          Two or more races\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         \xe2\x80\x93\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         \xe2\x80\x93\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         2.5%\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         2.7%\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Non-Hispanic_Whites" title="Non-Hispanic Whites">\n        Non-Hispanic Whites\n       </a>\n       were 58.9% of the population in 2011,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NJCensusfacts_67-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NJCensusfacts-67">\n         [67]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       down from 85% in 1970.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-68">\n        <a href="#cite_note-68">\n         [68]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In 2010, undocumented immigrants constituted an estimated 6.4% of the population. This was the fourth highest percentage of any state in the country.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-69">\n        <a href="#cite_note-69">\n         [69]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       There were an estimated 550,000 illegal immigrants in the state in 2010.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-70">\n        <a href="#cite_note-70">\n         [70]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States_Census_Bureau" title="United States Census Bureau">\n        United States Census Bureau\n       </a>\n       , as of July 1, 2015\n       <sup class="plainlinks noprint asof-tag update" style="display:none;">\n        <a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=New_Jersey&amp;action=edit">\n         [update]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       , estimated New Jersey\'s population at 8,958,013,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-PopEstUS_63-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-PopEstUS-63">\n         [63]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       which represents an increase of 166,119, or 1.89%, since the last census in 2010. This includes a natural increase since the last census of 343,965 people (that is, 933,185 births minus 589,220 deaths) and a decrease due to net migration of 53,930 people out of the state.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-census_cum_71-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-census_cum-71">\n         [71]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/Immigration_to_the_United_States" title="Immigration to the United States">\n        Immigration\n       </a>\n       from outside the United States resulted in a net increase of 384,687 people, and migration within the country produced a net loss of 438,617 people.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-census_cum_71-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-census_cum-71">\n         [71]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       As of 2005\n       <sup class="plainlinks noprint asof-tag update" style="display:none;">\n        <a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=New_Jersey&amp;action=edit">\n         [update]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       , there were 1.6 million foreign-born living in the state (accounting for 19.2% of the population).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-72">\n        <a href="#cite_note-72">\n         [72]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       As of 2010, New Jersey is the eleventh-most populous state in the United States, and the most densely populated, at 1,185 residents per square mile (458 per km\n       <sup>\n        2\n       </sup>\n       ), with most of the population residing in the counties surrounding New York City, Philadelphia, and along the eastern\n       <a href="/wiki/Jersey_Shore" title="Jersey Shore">\n        Jersey Shore\n       </a>\n       , while the extreme southern and northwestern counties are relatively less dense overall. It is also the second wealthiest state according to the U.S. Census Bureau.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NJMedianIncome_20-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NJMedianIncome-20">\n         [20]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/Center_of_population" title="Center of population">\n        center of population\n       </a>\n       for New Jersey is located in\n       <a href="/wiki/Middlesex_County,_New_Jersey" title="Middlesex County, New Jersey">\n        Middlesex County\n       </a>\n       , in the town of\n       <a href="/wiki/Milltown,_New_Jersey" title="Milltown, New Jersey">\n        Milltown\n       </a>\n       , just east of the\n       <a href="/wiki/New_Jersey_Turnpike" title="New Jersey Turnpike">\n        New Jersey Turnpike\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-73">\n        <a href="#cite_note-73">\n         [73]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       New Jersey is home to more\n       <a href="/wiki/Scientist" title="Scientist">\n        scientists\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Engineer" title="Engineer">\n        engineers\n       </a>\n       per square mile than anywhere else in the world.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-74">\n        <a href="#cite_note-74">\n         [74]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-75">\n        <a href="#cite_note-75">\n         [75]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-76">\n        <a href="#cite_note-76">\n         [76]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       On October 21, 2013,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Recognition_of_same-sex_unions_in_New_Jersey" title="Recognition of same-sex unions in New Jersey">\n        same-sex marriages\n       </a>\n       commenced in New Jersey.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-DroppedAppeal_77-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-DroppedAppeal-77">\n         [77]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       New Jersey is one of the most ethnically and religiously\n       <a href="/wiki/Polyethnicity" title="Polyethnicity">\n        diverse\n       </a>\n       states in the country. As of 2011, 56.4% of New Jersey\'s children under the age of one belonged to racial or ethnic minority groups, meaning that they had at least one parent who was not non-Hispanic white.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-78">\n        <a href="#cite_note-78">\n         [78]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       It has the second largest\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Jewish_American" title="Jewish American">\n        Jewish\n       </a>\n       population by percentage (after New York);\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-79">\n        <a href="#cite_note-79">\n         [79]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       the second largest\n       <a href="/wiki/Islam_in_the_United_States" title="Islam in the United States">\n        Muslim\n       </a>\n       population by percentage (after\n       <a href="/wiki/Michigan" title="Michigan">\n        Michigan\n       </a>\n       ); the largest population of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Peruvian_American" title="Peruvian American">\n        Peruvian Americans\n       </a>\n       in the United States; the largest population of\n       <a href="/wiki/Cuban_Americans" title="Cuban Americans">\n        Cubans\n       </a>\n       outside of Florida; the third highest\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Asian_American" title="Asian American">\n        Asian\n       </a>\n       population by percentage; and the third highest\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Italian-American" title="Italian-American">\n        Italian\n       </a>\n       population by percentage, according to the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_States_2000_Census" title="United States 2000 Census">\n        2000 Census\n       </a>\n       . African Americans,\n       <a href="/wiki/Hispanic_and_Latino_Americans" title="Hispanic and Latino Americans">\n        Hispanics\n       </a>\n       (\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Puerto_Rican_American" title="Puerto Rican American">\n        Puerto Ricans\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Dominican_American" title="Dominican American">\n        Dominicans\n       </a>\n       ),\n       <a href="/wiki/West_Indian_Americans" title="West Indian Americans">\n        West Indians\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Arab_American" title="Arab American">\n        Arabs\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Brazilian_people" title="Brazilian people">\n        Brazilian\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Portuguese_Americans" title="Portuguese Americans">\n        Portuguese Americans\n       </a>\n       are also high in number. New Jersey has the third highest\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Indian_American#List_of_U.S._States_by_population_of_Asian_Indians" title="Indian American">\n        Asian Indian\n       </a>\n       population of any state by absolute numbers and the highest by percentage,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-80">\n        <a href="#cite_note-80">\n         [80]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-81">\n        <a href="#cite_note-81">\n         [81]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-82">\n        <a href="#cite_note-82">\n         [82]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-censusbrief_83-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-censusbrief-83">\n         [83]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       with\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bergen_County" title="Bergen County">\n        Bergen County\n       </a>\n       home to America\'s largest\n       <a href="/wiki/Malayali" title="Malayali">\n        Malayali\n       </a>\n       community.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-84">\n        <a href="#cite_note-84">\n         [84]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Overall, New Jersey has the third largest\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Korean_American" title="Korean American">\n        Korean\n       </a>\n       population, with Bergen County home to the highest Korean concentration per capita of any U.S. county\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Richard_Newman_85-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Richard_Newman-85">\n         [85]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       (6.9% in 2011). New Jersey also has the fourth largest\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Filipino_American" title="Filipino American">\n        Filipino\n       </a>\n       population, and fourth largest\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Chinese_American" title="Chinese American">\n        Chinese\n       </a>\n       population, per the 2010 U.S. Census. The five largest ethnic groups in 2000 were:\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Italian-American" title="Italian-American">\n        Italian\n       </a>\n       (17.9%),\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Irish_American" title="Irish American">\n        Irish\n       </a>\n       (15.9%),\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/African_American" title="African American">\n        African\n       </a>\n       (13.6%),\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/German_American" title="German American">\n        German\n       </a>\n       (12.6%),\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Polish_American" title="Polish American">\n        Polish\n       </a>\n       (6.9%).\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Newark was the fourth poorest of U.S. cities with over 250,000 residents in 2008,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-86">\n        <a href="#cite_note-86">\n         [86]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       but New Jersey as a whole had the second-highest\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Median_household_income" title="Median household income">\n        median household income\n       </a>\n       as of 2014.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NJMedianIncome_20-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NJMedianIncome-20">\n         [20]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       This is largely because so much of New Jersey consists of suburbs, most of them affluent, of New York City and\n       <a href="/wiki/Philadelphia" title="Philadelphia">\n        Philadelphia\n       </a>\n       . New Jersey is also the most densely populated state, and the only state that has had every one of its counties deemed "urban" as defined by the\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States_Census_Bureau" title="United States Census Bureau">\n        Census Bureau\n       </a>\n       \'s\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Combined_Statistical_Area" title="Combined Statistical Area">\n        Combined Statistical Area\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-87">\n        <a href="#cite_note-87">\n         [87]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Broad_Avenue_Palisades_Park.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2304" data-file-width="3072" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/92/Broad_Avenue_Palisades_Park.jpg/220px-Broad_Avenue_Palisades_Park.jpg" with significant Korean-American populations">\n          all of the nation\'s top ten municipalities by percentage of Korean population\n         </a>\n         , led by\n         <a href="/wiki/Koreatown,_Palisades_Park" title="Koreatown, Palisades Park">\n          Palisades Park\n         </a>\n         (above), a\n         <a href="/wiki/Borough_(New_Jersey)" title="Borough (New Jersey)">\n          borough\n         </a>\n         where\n         <a href="/wiki/Koreans" title="Koreans">\n          Koreans\n         </a>\n         comprise the majority (52%) of the population.\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-88">\n          <a href="#cite_note-88">\n           [88]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-89">\n          <a href="#cite_note-89">\n           [89]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div Square">\n          India Square\n         </a>\n         ,\n         <a href="/wiki/Jersey_City,_New_Jersey" title="Jersey City, New Jersey">\n          Jersey City\n         </a>\n         , known as\n         <i>\n          Little\n          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bombay" title="Bombay">\n           Bombay\n          </a>\n         </i>\n         ,\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-90">\n          <a href="#cite_note-90">\n           [90]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n         home to the highest concentration of\n         <a href="/wiki/Indians_in_the_New_York_City_metropolitan_region" title="Indians in the New York City metropolitan region">\n          Asian Indians\n         </a>\n         in the\n         <a the largest\n         <a href="/wiki/Foreign_born" title="Foreign born">\n          foreign-born\n         </a>\n         nationality in New Jersey in 2013.\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-IndiaNewJersey_92-0">\n          <a href="#cite_note-IndiaNewJersey-92">\n           [92]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:New_Jersey_Counties_by_metro_area_labeled.svg">\n         <img alt="" statistical areas and divisions of New Jersey\n         </a>\n         . The\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/New_York_City_Metropolitan_Area" title="New York City Metropolitan Area">\n          New York City Metropolitan Area\n         </a>\n         includes the counties shaded in blue hues, as well as\n         <a href="/wiki/Mercer_County,_New_Jersey" title="Mercer County, New Jersey">\n          Mercer\n         </a>\n         and\n         <a href="/wiki/Warren_County,_New_Jersey" title="Warren County, New Jersey">\n          Warren\n         </a>\n         counties, the latter representing part of the\n         <a href="/wiki/Lehigh_Valley" title="Lehigh Valley">\n          Lehigh Valley\n         </a>\n         . Counties shaded in green hues, as well as\n         <a href="/wiki/Atlantic_County,_New_Jersey" title="Atlantic County, New Jersey">\n          Atlantic\n         </a>\n         ,\n         <a href="/wiki/Cape_May_County,_New_Jersey" title="Cape May County, New Jersey">\n          Cape May\n         </a>\n         , and\n         <a href="/wiki/Cumberland_County,_New_Jersey" title="Cumberland County, New Jersey">\n          Cumberland\n         </a>\n         counties, belong to the\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Philadelphia_Metropolitan_Area" title="Philadelphia Metropolitan Area">\n          Philadelphia Metropolitan Area\n         </a>\n         .\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       In 2010, 6.2% of its population was reported as under age 5, 23.5% under 18, and 13.5% were 65 or older; and females made up approximately 51.3% of the population.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-93">\n        <a href="#cite_note-93">\n         [93]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       A study by the\n       <a href="/wiki/Pew_Research_Center" title="Pew Research Center">\n        Pew Research Center\n       </a>\n       found that in 2013, New Jersey was the only U.S. state in which immigrants born in\n       <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">\n        India\n       </a>\n       constituted the largest\n       <a href="/wiki/Foreign_born" title="Foreign born">\n        foreign-born\n       </a>\n       nationality, representing roughly 10% of all foreign-born residents in the state.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-IndiaNewJersey_92-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-IndiaNewJersey-92">\n         [92]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       For further information on various ethnic groups and neighborhoods prominently featured within New Jersey, see the following articles:\n      </p>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        <a class="mw-headline" id="Birth_data">\n        Birth data\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       As of 2011, 56.4% of New Jersey\'s population younger than age 1 were minorities (meaning that they had at least one parent who was not non-Hispanic white).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-94">\n        <a href="#cite_note-94">\n         [94]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n   <td>\n         <b>\n          103,127\n         </b>\n         (100%)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Languages">\n        Languages\n    0.56%\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       As of 2010, 71.31% (5,830,812) of New Jersey residents age 5 and older spoke\n       <a href="/wiki/English_language" title="English language">\n        English\n       </a>\n       at home as a\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Primary_language" title="Primary language">\n        primary language\n       </a>\n       , while 14.59% (1,193,261) spoke\n       <a href="/wiki/Spanish_language" title="Spanish language">\n        Spanish\n       </a>\n       , 1.23% (100,217)\n       <a href="/wiki/Chinese_language" title="Chinese language">\n        Chinese\n       </a>\n       (which includes\n       <a href="/wiki/Cantonese" title="Cantonese">\n        Cantonese\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Standard_Chinese" title="Standard Chinese">\n        Mandarin\n       </a>\n       ), 1.06% (86,849)\n       <a href="/wiki/Italian_language" title="Italian language">\n        Italian\n       </a>\n       , 1.06% (86,486)\n       <a href="/wiki/Portuguese_language" title="Portuguese language">\n        Portuguese\n       </a>\n       , 0.96% (78,627)\n       <a href="/wiki/Tagalog_language" title="Tagalog language">\n        Tagalog\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Korean_language" title="Korean language">\n        Korean\n       </a>\n       was spoken as a\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Main_language" title="Main language">\n        main language\n       </a>\n       by 0.89% (73,057) of the population over the age of five. In total, 28.69% (2,345,644) of New Jersey\'s population age 5 and older spoke a\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mother_language" title="Mother language">\n        mother language\n       </a>\n       other than English.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-MLA_Data_98-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-MLA_Data-98">\n         [98]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       A diverse collection of languages has since evolved amongst the state\'s population, given that New Jersey has become\n       <a href="/wiki/Multiculturalism" title="Multiculturalism">\n        cosmopolitan\n       </a>\n       and is home to\n       <a href="/wiki/Ethnic_enclave" title="Ethnic enclave">\n        ethnic enclaves\n       </a>\n       of non-English-speaking communities:\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-99">\n        <a href="#cite_note-99">\n         [99]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-100">\n New Jersey is home to the second-highest\n          <a href="/wiki/American_Jews#Demographics" title="American Jews">\n           Jewish American\n          </a>\n          (\n          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hebrew" title="Hebrew">\n           Hebrew\n          </a>\n          ) population per capita, after\n          <a href="/wiki/New_York_(state)" title="New York (state)">\n           New York\n          </a>\n          .\n         </div>\n        </div>\n        <div class="tsingle" style="float:left;margin:1px;width:252px;max-width:252px">\n         <div class="thumbimage">\n          <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:BAPS_Robbinsville_Mandir_-_Exterior.jpg">\n           <img alt="" data-file-height="721" data-file-width="1198" height="150" <div class="thumbcaption" style="clear:left">\n          <a href="/wiki/Akshardham_(New_Jersey)" title="Akshardham (New Jersey)">\n           Swaminarayan Akshardham\n          </a>\n          (\n          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Devnagari" title="Devnagari">\n           Devnagari\n          </a>\n          ) in\n          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Robbinsville,_New_Jersey" title="Robbinsville, New Jersey">\n           Robbinsville\n          </a>\n          ,\n          <a href="/wiki/Mercer_County,_New_Jersey" title="Mercer County, New Jersey">\n           Mercer County\n          </a>\n          , inaugurated in 2014 as the world\'s largest\n          <a href="/wiki/Hindu_temple" title="Hindu temple">\n           Hindu temple\n          </a>\n          .\n          <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-World.27sLargestHinduTempleNJ_109-0">\n           <a href="#cite_note-World.27sLargestHinduTempleNJ-109">\n            [109]\n           </a>\n          </sup>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n        <div class="tsingle" style="float:left;margin:1px;width:197px;max-width:197px">\n         <div class="thumbimage">\n          <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Iftar_in_Patterson_New_Jersey.jpg">\n           <img alt="" data-file-height="401" data-file-width="500" height="156" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fc/Iftar_in_Patterson_New_Jersey.jpg/195px-Iftar_in_Patterson_New_Jersey.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fc/Iftar_in_Patterson_New_Jersey.jpg/293px-Iftar_in_Patterson_New_Jersey.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fc/Iftar_in_Patterson_New_Jersey.jpg/390px-Iftar_in_Patterson_New_Jersey.jpg 2x" width="195"/>\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <div class="thumbcaption" style="clear:left">\n          <i>\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Little_Ramallah" title="Little Ramallah">\n            Little Ramallah\n           </a>\n          </i>\n          in\n          <a href="/wiki/Paterson,_New_Jersey" title="Paterson, New Jersey">\n           Paterson\n          </a>\n          is an increasingly popular destination for\n          <a href="/wiki/Muslim" title="Muslim">\n           Muslim\n          </a>\n          immigrants.\n          <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-PatersonSocSec_110-0">\n           <a href="#cite_note-PatersonSocSec-110">\n            [110]\n           </a>\n          </sup>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n        <div style="clear:left">\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       By number of adherents, the largest denominations in New Jersey, according to the\n       <a href="/wiki/Association_of_Religion_Data_Archives" title="Association of Religion Data Archives">\n        Association of Religion Data Archives\n       </a>\n       in 2010, were the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Church" title="Roman Catholic Church">\n        Roman Catholic Church\n       </a>\n       with 3,235,290;\n       <a href="/wiki/Islam" title="Islam">\n        Islam\n       </a>\n       with 160,666; and the\n       <a href="/wiki/United_Methodist_Church" title="United Methodist Church">\n        United Methodist Church\n       </a>\n       with 138,052.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-www.thearda.com_111-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-www.thearda.com-111">\n         [111]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The world\'s largest\n       <a href="/wiki/Hindu_temple" title="Hindu temple">\n        Hindu temple\n       </a>\n       was inaugurated in\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Robbinsville,_New_Jersey" title="Robbinsville, New Jersey">\n        Robbinsville\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Mercer_County,_New_Jersey" title="Mercer County, New Jersey">\n        Mercer County\n       </a>\n       , in\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Central_New_Jersey" title="Central New Jersey">\n        central New Jersey\n       </a>\n       during 2014, a\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/BAPS" title="BAPS">\n        BAPS\n       </a>\n       temple.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-112">\n        <a href="#cite_note-112">\n         [112]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Settlements">\n        Settlements\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       See also:\n       <a New Jersey\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       For its overall population and nation-leading population density, New Jersey has a relative paucity of classic large cities. This paradox is most pronounced in\n       <a href="/wiki/Bergen_County,_New_Jersey" title="Bergen County, New Jersey">\n        Bergen County\n       </a>\n       , New Jersey\'s most populous county, whose more than 930,000 residents in 2014 inhabited 70 municipalities, the most populous being\n       <a href="/wiki/Hackensack,_New_Jersey" title="Hackensack, New Jersey">\n        Hackensack\n       </a>\n       , with 44,519 residents estimated in 2014. Many urban areas extend far beyond the limits of a single large city, as New Jersey cities (and indeed municipalities in general) tend to be geographically small; three of the four largest cities in New Jersey by population have under 20 square miles of land area, and eight of the top ten, including all of the top five have land area under 30 square miles. As of the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_States_2010_Census" title="United States 2010 Census">\n        United States 2010 Census\n       </a>\n       <sup class="plainlinks noprint asof-tag update" style="display:none;">\n        <a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=New_Jersey&amp;action=edit">\n         [update]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       , only four municipalities had populations in excess of 100,000, although Edison and Woodbridge came very close.\n      </p>\n      <table class="wikitable sortable collapsible
