 </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Jersey_Shore">\n        Jersey Shore\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Jersey_Shore" title="Jersey Shore">\n        Jersey Shore\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tnone" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right:auto; overflow:hidden; width:auto; max-width:908px;">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="">\n        <div class="overflowbugx" style="overflow:auto;">\n         <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Belmar-panorama.jpg" title="Belmar, on the Jersey Shore.">\n          <img alt="" data-file-height="272" data-file-width="1376" height="178" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2e/Belmar-panorama.jpg/900px-Belmar-panorama.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2e/Belmar-panorama.jpg/1350px-Belmar-panorama.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/2/2e/Belmar-panorama.jpg 2x" width="900"/>\n         </a>\n        </div>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a href="/wiki/File:Belmar-panorama.jpg" title="File:Belmar-panorama.jpg">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <a href="/wiki/Belmar,_New_Jersey" title="Belmar, New Jersey">\n          Belmar\n         </a>\n         , on the Jersey Shore.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Culture">\n        Culture\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="General">\n        General\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Like every state, New Jersey has its own\n       <a href="/wiki/Cuisine_of_New_Jersey" title="Cuisine of New Jersey">\n        cuisine\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Religion_in_New_Jersey" title="Religion in New Jersey">\n        religious communities\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/List_of_museums_in_New_Jersey" title="List of museums in New Jersey">\n        museums\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Category:Halls_of_fame_in_New_Jersey" title="Category:Halls of fame in New Jersey">\n        halls of fame\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       New Jersey is the birthplace of modern inventions such as:\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/FM_radio" title="FM radio">\n        FM radio\n       </a>\n       , the motion picture camera, the\n       <a href="/wiki/Lithium_battery" title="Lithium battery">\n        lithium battery\n       </a>\n       , the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Light_bulb" title="Light bulb">\n        light bulb\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Transistor" title="Transistor">\n        transistors\n       </a>\n       , and the electric train. Other New Jersey creations include: the drive-in movie, the cultivated\n       <a href="/wiki/Blueberry" title="Blueberry">\n        blueberry\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Cranberry_sauce" title="Cranberry sauce">\n        cranberry sauce\n       </a>\n       , the postcard, the\n       <a href="/wiki/Boardwalk" title="Boardwalk">\n        boardwalk\n       </a>\n       , the\n       <a href="/wiki/Zipper" title="Zipper">\n        zipper\n       </a>\n       , the\n       <a href="/wiki/Phonograph" title="Phonograph">\n        phonograph\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Saltwater_taffy" title="Saltwater taffy">\n        saltwater taffy\n       </a>\n       , the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Dirigible" title="Dirigible">\n        dirigible\n       </a>\n       , the\n       <a href="/wiki/Watermelon" title="Watermelon">\n        seedless watermelon\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-177">\n        <a href="#cite_note-177">\n         [177]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       the\n       <a href="/wiki/David_Bushnell" title="David Bushnell">\n        first use\n       </a>\n       of a\n       <a href="/wiki/Submarine" title="Submarine">\n        submarine\n       </a>\n       in warfare, and the\n       <a href="/wiki/Ice_cream_cone" title="Ice cream cone">\n        ice cream cone\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-178">\n        <a href="#cite_note-178">\n         [178]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:A_50%27s_Style_Diner.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1350" data-file-width="2048" height="145" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0a/A_50%27s_Style_Diner.jpg/220px-A_50%27s_Style_Diner.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0a/A_50%27s_Style_Diner.jpg/330px-A_50%27s_Style_Diner.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0a/A_50%27s_Style_Diner.jpg/440px-A_50%27s_Style_Diner.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:A_50%27s_Style_Diner.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         A 1950s-style diner in\n         <a href="/wiki/Orange,_New_Jersey" title="Orange, New Jersey">\n          Orange\n         </a>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       There are mineral museums in Franklin and Ogdensburg.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       <a href="/wiki/Diner" title="Diner">\n        Diners\n       </a>\n       are common in New Jersey. The state is home to many diner manufacturers and has more diners than any other state: over 600. There are more diners in the state of New Jersey than any other place in the world.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-179">\n        <a href="#cite_note-179">\n         [179]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       New Jersey is the only state without a state song.\n       <i>\n        I\'m From New Jersey\n       </i>\n       is incorrectly listed on many websites as being the New Jersey state song, but it was not even a contender when in 1996 the New Jersey Arts Council submitted their suggestions to the\n       <a href="/wiki/New_Jersey_Legislature" title="New Jersey Legislature">\n        New Jersey Legislature\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-180">\n        <a href="#cite_note-180">\n         [180]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       New Jersey is frequently the target of jokes in American culture,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-181">\n        <a href="#cite_note-181">\n         [181]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       especially from\n       <a href="/wiki/New_York_City" title="New York City">\n        New York City\n       </a>\n       -based television shows, such as\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/Saturday_Night_Live" title="Saturday Night Live">\n         Saturday Night Live\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       . Academic\n       <a href="/wiki/Michael_Aaron_Rockland" title="Michael Aaron Rockland">\n        Michael Aaron Rockland\n       </a>\n       attributes this to New Yorkers\' view that New Jersey is the beginning of\n       <a href="/wiki/Middle_America_(United_States)" title="Middle America (United States)">\n        Middle America\n       </a>\n       . The\n       <a href="/wiki/New_Jersey_Turnpike" title="New Jersey Turnpike">\n        New Jersey Turnpike\n       </a>\n       , which runs between two major East Coast cities, New York City and\n       <a href="/wiki/Philadelphia" title="Philadelphia">\n        Philadelphia\n       </a>\n       , is also cited as a reason, as people who traverse through the state may only see its industrial zones.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-sjt_182-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-sjt-182">\n         [182]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Reality television shows like\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/Jersey_Shore_(TV_series)" title="Jersey Shore (TV series)">\n         Jersey Shore\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       and\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/The_Real_Housewives_of_New_Jersey" title="The Real Housewives of New Jersey">\n         The Real Housewives of New Jersey\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       have reinforced stereotypical views of New Jersey culture,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-183">\n        <a href="#cite_note-183">\n         [183]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       but Rockland cited\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/The_Sopranos" title="The Sopranos">\n         The Sopranos\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       and the music of Bruce Springsteen as exporting a more positive image.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-sjt_182-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-sjt-182">\n         [182]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Cuisine">\n        Cuisine\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Cuisine_of_New_Jersey" title="Cuisine of New Jersey">\n        Cuisine of New Jersey\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       New Jersey is known for several foods developed within the region, including\n       <a href="/wiki/Pork_roll" title="Pork roll">\n        pork roll\n       </a>\n       (or Taylor ham),\n       <a href="/wiki/Cheesesteak" title="Cheesesteak">\n        cheesesteaks\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Scrapple" title="Scrapple">\n        scrapple\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Credit for the development of\n       <a href="/wiki/Submarine_sandwich" title="Submarine sandwich">\n        submarine sandwiches\n       </a>\n       is claimed by several states with substantial Italian American populations, including New Jersey.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-184">\n        <a href="#cite_note-184">\n         [184]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Music">\n        Music\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Music_of_New_Jersey" title="Music of New Jersey">\n        Music of New Jersey\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       New Jersey has long been an important area for both\n       <a href="/wiki/Rock_and_roll" title="Rock and roll">\n        rock\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Hip_hop_music" title="Hip hop music">\n        rap\n       </a>\n       music. Some prominent musicians from or with significant connections to New Jersey are:\n      </p>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        Singer\n        <a href="/wiki/Frank_Sinatra" title="Frank Sinatra">\n         Frank Sinatra\n        </a>\n        was born in\n        <a href="/wiki/Hoboken,_New_Jersey" title="Hoboken, New Jersey">\n         Hoboken\n        </a>\n        . He sang with a neighborhood vocal group, the Hoboken Four, and appeared in neighborhood theater amateur shows before he became an\n        <a href="/wiki/Academy_Awards" title="Academy Awards">\n         Academy Award\n        </a>\n        \xe2\x80\x93winning actor.\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Bruce_Springsteen" title="Bruce Springsteen">\n         Bruce Springsteen\n        </a>\n        , who has sung of New Jersey life on most of his albums, is from\n        <a href="/wiki/Freehold_Borough,_New_Jersey" title="Freehold Borough, New Jersey">\n         Freehold\n        </a>\n        . Some of his songs that represent New Jersey life are "\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Born_to_Run_(song)" title="Born to Run (song)">\n         Born to Run\n        </a>\n        ", "Spirit In The Night," "\n        <a href="/wiki/Rosalita_(Come_Out_Tonight)" title="Rosalita (Come Out Tonight)">\n         Rosalita (Come Out Tonight)\n        </a>\n        ", "\n        <a href="/wiki/Thunder_Road_(song)" title="Thunder Road (song)">\n         Thunder Road\n        </a>\n        ", "\n        <a href="/wiki/Atlantic_City_(song)" title="Atlantic City (song)">\n         Atlantic City\n        </a>\n        ", and "\n        <a href="/wiki/Jungleland" title="Jungleland">\n         Jungleland\n        </a>\n        ".\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        The\n        <a href="/wiki/Jonas_Brothers" title="Jonas Brothers">\n         Jonas Brothers\n        </a>\n        all reside in Wyckoff, New Jersey, where the eldest and youngest brothers of the group, Kevin and Frankie Jonas, were born.\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Irvington,_New_Jersey" title="Irvington, New Jersey">\n         Irvington\n        </a>\n        \'s\n        <a href="/wiki/Queen_Latifah" title="Queen Latifah">\n         Queen Latifah\n        </a>\n        was the first female rapper to succeed in music, film, and television.\n        <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">\n         [\n         <i>\n          <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">\n           <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (July 2014)">\n            citation needed\n           </span>\n          </a>\n         </i>\n         ]\n        </sup>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Lauryn_Hill" title="Lauryn Hill">\n         Lauryn Hill\n        </a>\n        is from\n        <a href="/wiki/South_Orange,_New_Jersey" title="South Orange, New Jersey">\n         South Orange, New Jersey\n        </a>\n        . Her 1998 debut solo album,\n        <i>\n         <a href="/wiki/The_Miseducation_of_Lauryn_Hill" title="The Miseducation of Lauryn Hill">\n          The Miseducation of Lauryn Hill\n         </a>\n        </i>\n        , sold 10 million copies internationally.\n        <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">\n         [\n         <i>\n          <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">\n           <span title="unless this has something to do with NJ, the name should be omitted (July 2014)">\n            citation needed\n           </span>\n          </a>\n         </i>\n         ]\n        </sup>\n        She also sold millions with\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/The_Fugees" title="The Fugees">\n         The Fugees\n        </a>\n        second album\n        <i>\n         <a href="/wiki/The_Score_(Fugees_album)" title="The Score (Fugees album)">\n          The Score\n         </a>\n        </i>\n        .\n        <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">\n         [\n         <i>\n          <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">\n           <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (July 2014)">\n            citation needed\n           </span>\n          </a>\n         </i>\n         ]\n        </sup>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Southside_Johnny" title="Southside Johnny">\n         Southside Johnny\n        </a>\n        , eponymous leader of Southside Johnny and the Asbury Jukes was raised in\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ocean_Grove,_NJ" title="Ocean Grove, NJ">\n         Ocean Grove\n        </a>\n        . He is considered the "Grandfather of the New Jersey Sound"\n        <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">\n         [\n         <i>\n          <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">\n           <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (July 2014)">\n            citation needed\n           </span>\n          </a>\n         </i>\n         ]\n        </sup>\n        and is cited by Jersey-born\n        <a href="/wiki/Jon_Bon_Jovi" title="Jon Bon Jovi">\n         Jon Bon Jovi\n        </a>\n        as his reason for singing.\n        <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">\n         [\n         <i>\n          <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">\n           <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (July 2014)">\n            citation needed\n           </span>\n          </a>\n         </i>\n         ]\n        </sup>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Redman_(rapper)" title="Redman (rapper)">\n         Redman\n        </a>\n        (Reggie Noble) was born, raised, and resides in\n        <a href="/wiki/Newark,_New_Jersey" title="Newark, New Jersey">\n         Newark\n        </a>\n        . He is the most successful African-American solo hip-hop artist out of New Jersey.\n        <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">\n         [\n         <i>\n          <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">\n           <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (July 2014)">\n            citation needed\n           </span>\n          </a>\n         </i>\n         ]\n        </sup>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        All members of\n        <a href="/wiki/The_Sugarhill_Gang" title="The Sugarhill Gang">\n         The Sugarhill Gang\n        </a>\n        were born in\n        <a href="/wiki/Englewood,_New_Jersey" title="Englewood, New Jersey">\n         Englewood\n        </a>\n        .\n        <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">\n         [\n         <i>\n          <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">\n           <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (July 2014)">\n            citation needed\n           </span>\n          </a>\n         </i>\n         ]\n        </sup>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Roc-A-Fella_Records" title="Roc-A-Fella Records">\n         Roc-A-Fella Records\n        </a>\n        rap producer\n        <a href="/wiki/Just_Blaze" title="Just Blaze">\n         Just Blaze\n        </a>\n        is from\n        <a href="/wiki/Paterson,_New_Jersey" title="Paterson, New Jersey">\n         Paterson, New Jersey\n        </a>\n        .\n        <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">\n         [\n         <i>\n          <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">\n           <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (July 2014)">\n            citation needed\n           </span>\n          </a>\n         </i>\n         ]\n        </sup>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Jon_Bon_Jovi" title="Jon Bon Jovi">\n         Jon Bon Jovi\n        </a>\n        , from\n        <a href="/wiki/Sayreville,_New_Jersey" title="Sayreville, New Jersey">\n         Sayreville\n        </a>\n        , reached fame in the 1980s with hard rock outfit\n        <a href="/wiki/Bon_Jovi" title="Bon Jovi">\n         Bon Jovi\n        </a>\n        . The band has also written many songs about life in New Jersey including "Livin\' On A Prayer"\n        <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">\n         [\n         <i>\n          <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">\n           <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. </a>\n         , home of the MLS\'s New York Red Bulls\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/National_Hockey_League" title="National Hockey League">\n        National Hockey League\n       </a>\n       \'s\n       <a href="/wiki/New_Jersey_Devils" title="New Jersey Devils">\n        New Jersey Devils\n       </a>\n       , based in Newark at the\n       <a href="/wiki/Prudential_Center" title="Prudential Center">\n        Prudential Center\n       </a>\n       , is the only major league franchise to bear the state\'s name. The Metropolitan Area\'s two\n       <a href="/wiki/National_Football_League" title="National Football League">\n        National Football League\n       </a>\n       teams, the\n       <a href="/wiki/New_York_Giants" title="New York Giants">\n        New York Giants\n       </a>\n       and the\n       <a href="/wiki/New_York_Jets" title="New York Jets">\n        New York Jets\n       </a>\n       , both play in\n       <a href="/wiki/East_Rutherford,_New_Jersey" title="East Rutherford, New Jersey">\n        East Rutherford\n       </a>\n       , Bergen County, at\n       <a href="/wiki/MetLife_Stadium" title="MetLife Stadium">\n        MetLife Stadium\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-194">\n        <a href="#cite_note-194">\n         [194]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Completed at a cost of approximately $1.6 billion\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Belson_195-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Belson-195">\n         [195]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       it is the most expensive stadium ever built.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Esteban_193-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Esteban-193">\n         [193]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On February 2, 2014, MetLife Stadium hosted\n       <a href="/wiki/Super_Bowl_XLVIII" title="Super Bowl XLVIII">\n        Super Bowl XLVIII\n       </a>\n       , the first Super Bowl played outdoors in a cold-weather city.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/New_York_Red_Bulls" title="New York Red Bulls">\n        New York Red Bulls\n       </a>\n       of\n       <a href="/wiki/Major_League_Soccer" title="Major League Soccer">\n        Major League Soccer\n       </a>\n       play in\n       <a href="/wiki/Red_Bull_Arena_(New_Jersey)" title="Red Bull Arena (New Jersey)">\n        Red Bull Arena\n       </a>\n       , a soccer-specific stadium located in\n       <a href="/wiki/Harrison,_New_Jersey" title="Harrison, New Jersey">\n        Harrison\n       </a>\n       outside of downtown\n       <a href="/wiki/Newark,_New_Jersey" title="Newark, New Jersey">\n        Newark\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The sports complex is also home to the\n       <a href="/wiki/Meadowlands_Racetrack" title="Meadowlands Racetrack">\n        Meadowlands Racetrack\n       </a>\n       , one of three major\n       <a href="/wiki/Harness_racing" title="Harness racing">\n        harness racing\n       </a>\n       tracks in the state. The Meadowlands Racetrack along with\n       <a href="/wiki/Freehold_Raceway" title="Freehold Raceway">\n        Freehold Raceway\n       </a>\n       in Freehold are two of the major harness racing tracks in North America.\n       <a href="/wiki/Monmouth_Park_Racetrack" title="Monmouth Park Racetrack">\n        Monmouth Park Racetrack\n       </a>\n       in Oceanport is also a popular spot for\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Thoroughbred_racing" title="Thoroughbred racing">\n        thoroughbred racing\n       </a>\n       in New Jersey and the northeast. It hosted the\n       <a href="/wiki/Breeders%27_Cup" title="Breeders\' Cup">\n        Breeders\' Cup\n       </a>\n       in 2007, and its turf course was renovated in preparation.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Additionally, New Jersey is home to two\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/MLB" title="MLB">\n        MLB\n       </a>\n       affiliated\n       <a href="/wiki/Minor_League_Baseball" title="Minor League Baseball">\n        Minor League Baseball\n       </a>\n       teams: the\n       <a href="/wiki/Trenton_Thunder" title="Trenton Thunder">\n        Trenton Thunder\n       </a>\n       (\n       <a href="/wiki/New_York_Yankees" title="New York Yankees">\n        New York Yankees\n       </a>\n       affiliate) and the\n       <a href="/wiki/Lakewood_BlueClaws" title="Lakewood BlueClaws">\n        Lakewood BlueClaws\n       </a>\n       (\n       <a href="/wiki/Philadelphia_Phillies" title="Philadelphia Phillies">\n        Philadelphia Phillies\n       </a>\n       affiliate).\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The following table shows the major league sports teams in the state:\n      </p>\n      <table class="wikitable class="mw-headline" id="College_sports">\n        College sports\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       See also:\n       <a href="/wiki/List_of_college_athletic_programs_in_New_Jersey" title="List of college athletic programs in New Jersey">\n        List of college athletic programs in New Jersey\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       New Jerseyans\' collegiate allegiances are predominantly split among the four major\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Division_I_(NCAA)" title="Division I (NCAA)">\n        NCAA Division I\n       </a>\n       programs in the state \xe2\x80\x93 the\n       <a href="/wiki/Rutgers_University#Athletics" title="Rutgers University">\n        Rutgers University\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/Rutgers_Scarlet_Knights" title="Rutgers Scarlet Knights">\n        Scarlet Knights\n       </a>\n       , the\n       <a href="/wiki/NJIT_Highlanders" title="NJIT Highlanders">\n        NJIT Highlanders\n       </a>\n       , the\n       <a href="/wiki/Seton_Hall_Pirates" title="Seton Hall Pirates">\n        Seton Hall University\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/Seton_Hall_Pirates" title="Seton Hall Pirates">\n        Pirates\n       </a>\n       , and the\n       <a href="/wiki/Princeton_University#Athletics" title="Princeton University">\n        Princeton University\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/Princeton_Tigers" title="Princeton Tigers">\n        Tigers\n       </a>\n       . Rutgers joined the\n       <a href="/wiki/Big_Ten_Conference" title="Big Ten Conference">\n        Big Ten Conference\n       </a>\n       in 2014.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Rutgers and Princeton have an intense rivalry \xe2\x80\x93 stemming from the\n       <a href="/wiki/1869_college_football_season" title="1869 college football season">\n        first intercollegiate football game\n       </a>\n       in 1869 \xe2\x80\x93 though the two schools have not met on the football field since 1980. They continue to play each other annually in other sports.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Rutgers, which fields 24 teams in various sports, is nationally known for its excellent football and women\'s basketball programs.\n       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">\n        [\n        <i>\n         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">\n          <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (May 2014)">\n           citation needed\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </i>\n        ]\n       </sup>\n       The university is planning an expansion to\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Rutgers_Stadium" title="Rutgers Stadium">\n        Rutgers Stadium\n       </a>\n       , and the teams play in\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Piscataway_Township,_New_Jersey" title="Piscataway Township, New Jersey">\n        Piscataway\n       </a>\n       , which is adjacent to the New Brunswick campus. The university also fields rising basketball and baseball programs.\n       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">\n        [\n        <i>\n         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">\n          <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (May 2014)">\n           citation needed\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </i>\n        ]\n       </sup>\n       Rutgers\' fan base is mostly derived from the western parts of the state and\n       <a href="/wiki/Middlesex_County,_New_Jersey" title="Middlesex County, New Jersey">\n        Middlesex County\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">\n        [\n        <i>\n         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">\n          <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (May 2014)">\n           citation needed\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </i>\n        ]\n       </sup>\n       and its alumni base is the largest in the state.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Seton Hall\'s basketball team has been one of the most storied programs in the Big East,\n       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">\n        [\n        <i>\n         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">\n          <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (May 2014)">\n           citation needed\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </i>\n        ]\n       </sup>\n       and it plays its home games at the\n       <a href="/wiki/Prudential_Center" title="Prudential Center">\n        Prudential Center\n       </a>\n       in\n       <a href="/wiki/Newark,_New_Jersey" title="Newark, New Jersey">\n        Newark\n       </a>\n       . The Pirates have support in the predominantly Roman Catholic areas of the northern part of the state and the\n       <a href="/wiki/Jersey_Shore" title="Jersey Shore">\n        Jersey Shore\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">\n        [\n        <i>\n         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">\n          <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (May 2014)">\n           citation needed\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </i>\n        ]\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="High-school_sports">\n        High-school sports\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <p>\n       New Jersey high schools are divided into divisions under the\n       <a href="/wiki/New_Jersey_State_Interscholastic_Athletic_Association" title="New Jersey State Interscholastic Athletic Association">\n        New Jersey State Interscholastic Athletic Association\n       </a>\n       .(NJSIAA)\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-196">\n        <a href="#cite_note-196">\n         [196]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       \'\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-197">\n        <a href="#cite_note-197">\n         [197]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Founded in 1918, the NJSIAA currently represents 22,000 schools, 330,000 coaches, and almost 4.5 million athletes. Sports are divided between 3 seasons (fall, winter, and spring).\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="State_symbols">\n        State symbols\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n </h2>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Further information:\n       <a href="/wiki/List_of_people_from_New_Jersey" title="List of people from New Jersey">\n        List of people from New Jersey\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="See_also">\n        See also\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div aria-label="Portals" class="noprint portal plainlist tright" role="navigation" style="margin:0.5em 0 0.5em 1em;border:solid #aaa 1px">\n       <ul
